<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разослать.html>разосла́ть</a> (19131)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разо-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razo-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слать.html>сла́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">slátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разослать.html>разосла́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razoslátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рассылать.html>рассыла́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to send <i>(about, round)</i>, to distribute, to circulate</li></ol>

***разочарование.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ние</a> (5746)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровать.html>разочарова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razočarovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razočarovánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочарование.html>разочарова́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>disappointment (emotion)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разочароваться.html>разочарова́ться</a> (15837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровать.html>разочарова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razočarovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочароваться.html>разочарова́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razočarovátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разочаро́вываться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be disappointed <i>(in smb; with smth)</i></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровывать.html>разочаро́вывать</a> (26191)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровать.html>разочарова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razočarovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровывать.html>разочаро́вывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razočaróvyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разочаровать.html>разочарова́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to disappoint, to underwhelm, to disillusion, to disenchant</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывать</a> (9212)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrabátyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work out, to elaborate, to develop, to design, to engineer, to devise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минздрав.html>минздра́ве</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывают</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровление.html>оздоровле́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:россиянин.html>россия́н</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V Minzdráve <b>razrabátyvajut</b> plan po ozdorovléniju rossiján.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Ministry of Health is <b>developing</b> a plan to improve the health of Russians.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exploit, to work up (<i>mining</i>)</li>
<li>to cultivate, to till</li>
<li>to exhaust, to use up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатываться.html>разраба́тываться</a> (21160)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrabátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатываться.html>разраба́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrabátyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разрабо́таться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to begin to work with a zest, to get involved with one's work</li>
<li>to begin to work/run smoothly</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrabátyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разработать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тать</a> (4050)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:работать.html>рабо́тать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rabótatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrabótatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрабатывать.html>разраба́тывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to work out, to elaborate, to develop, to design, to engineer, to devise
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:минздрав.html>минздра́ве</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разработать.html>разрабо́тали</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:план.html>план</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оздоровление.html>оздоровле́нию</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:россиянин.html>россия́н</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">V Minzdráve <b>razrabótali</b> plan po ozdorovléniju rossiján.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The Ministry of Health <b>developed</b> a plan to improve the health of Russians.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to exploit, to work up (<i>mining</i>)</li>
<li>to cultivate, to till</li>
<li>to exhaust, to use up</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разработка.html>разрабо́тка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrabótka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разраба́тывание</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrabátyvanije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разработчик.html>разрабо́тчик</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrabótčik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разрабо́тчица</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razrabótčica</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разразиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разразиться.html>разрази́ться</a> (7656)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разрази́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разразиться.html>разрази́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrazítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разражаться.html>разража́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><i>(war, storm etc.)</i> to break out, to burst out</li>
<li>to burst <i>(into)</i>, to burst <i>(out)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разразиться.html>разрази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слеза.html>слеза́ми</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razrazítʹsja</b> slezámi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to burst into tears</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разразиться.html>разрази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:брань.html>бра́нью</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razrazítʹsja</b> bránʹju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to break into abuse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разразиться.html>разрази́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:смех.html>сме́хом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razrazítʹsja</b> sméxom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to burst out laughing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разрази́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrazítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***разрастание.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрастание.html>разраста́ние</a> (23910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">разраста́ть(ся)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razrastátʹ(sja)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастание.html>разраста́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrastánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастание.html>разраста́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастание.html>разраста́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастание.html>разраста́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>expansion, spreading, sprawl</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разрасти́сь</a> (13006)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разрасти́сь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrastísʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастаться.html>разраста́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to grow, to expand, to spread <i>(out)</i>, to grow thick, to bush out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́род</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быстро.html>бы́стро</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разро́сся</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">górod býstro <b>razróssja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the town has mushroomed</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́рево</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разросло́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dérevo <b>razroslósʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the tree has spread</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:роща.html>ро́ща</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разросла́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">róšča <b>razroslásʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the grove has grown thick</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:предприятие.html>предприя́тие</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разрастись.html>разросло́сь</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">predprijátije <b>razroslósʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the business/enterprise has grown/expanded</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:расти.html>расти́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rastí</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вырасти.html>вы́расти</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výrasti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***разрез.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрез.html>разре́з</a> (9884)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрез.html>разре́з</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razréz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрез.html>разре́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрез.html>разре́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрез.html>разре́зов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cut</li>
<li>section (cutting)</li>
<li>open-pit mine, strip mine</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разреза́ть</a> (7070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разре́зать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razrézatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:разрезать.html>разреза́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to cut off, to bisect</li></ol>
